* UPDATE IN RED BELOW ORIGINAL POST

Hi

This thread will focus on using the MTF(Multiple Time Frame) Stochastic.

This thread draws its inspiration from the Genesis Matrix System (http://www.forexfactory.com/showthread.php?t=373796 )

Thanks to RJ and the others for letting us start this Thread where we will focus on all variations of their 1 min System.

Please feel free to post all relevant 1 min charts here that you wish to share.Together with any description that you might feel useful in explaining why did what you did.

This not the place to have long winded debates and arguments about who's system or settings are better than the other.EACH TO THEIR OWN

I really hope we all can share what we use here and I for one am looking forward to share my trades as well as learning from others and improving myself.

Good luck and Good Trading

Rooi

Please remember that this is a 1min thread and that you can find the basics of the systems discussed here in the Genesis Matrix System thread.

10 / 09 / 2014

So after a lot of work on this system and myself in the last 9 months it only vaguely resembles the original version posted here in the beginning

This method has moved closer to the the Genesis method using everything like the original setup excluding the Stochastic. Proving that modeling something that is already working is much better than building a new.

The newest version is available on post  ( http://www.forexfactory.com/showthre...91#post7749891 )

For the first 133 pages please focus on Strada's views and trades as I trade very very similar to him now and that has always been the/my overall goal.
From page 133 I read the system much like he does.At least I hope

No need to read through everything.If you are really interested then please download everything you need from the Genesis Thread and ask if you need anything specific that is not yet provided in the thread that you might see me or someone else using here.

I WILL UPDATE HERE WHEN I STOP

TRADING THIS SYSTEM
So unless stated I am trading this system everyday

--- 帖子 #27 ---
Glad you asked that was a hasty post back there came back and saw that the market had hit mt SL a second time.

You see with multi time framing you can view several time frames on just one chart and have a feel of what is going on in each.

The screenshot below shows 5 different time frames in the M1 chart.

During news, if your brokers servers are very efficient, you have decent internet speed, and your pc has a high processor speed (I'm gonna have to get me a core i9 soon), you can trade in one minute, I have caught some decent pips during news time, all it takes is to wait for the initial reaction to abate and look for a retracement into your equilibrium MA for me that's the M5 trend, when that is coupled with a divergence, then you can ride out the remaining of the news spike.

Sometimes the trend reverses completely but if it doesn't like 8/10 with GBPUSD you can trade it.

Too busy trying to tidy my desk on my day job so I can go on vacation I'd have caught that retracement.

Let me know if you need further clarification.

--- 帖子 #29 ---
As we know, stochastics go OB / OS and can stay there for some time, during which time they are of less value.   Even moving up a TF as I have on this chart to the 4 hour does not help a lot.

I prefer to look at the PA around both levels and the known times.....this afternoon's rally started ~ the first NY Open, the US data at 13:30 cause that wide spike up.   Today, the open of the NYSE had no efffect - unlike the NY Cut at 10am EST / 15:00 GMT and the high was 7 minutes before price fell into the London Fix and we can expect further movement in the 16:30 - 17:00 gmt period....

--- 帖子 #32 ---
Good Morning Figgsey

Many may argue with me however in my personal opinion I don't consider Genesis 1 minute trading as scalping. The reason for trading on 1 minute charts is to be able to get into the market at a cheap SL and so as to capture as much of the move as possible. An entry that starts with a 1minute chart set up could go to be on the table for several hours.

Having said that I am not doubting that scalpers use 1 minute charts, but that's not the style of trading that Genesis is all about.

Just my thoughts and I would welcome comments.

Kind Regards

Anthm

--- 帖子 #33 ---
I totally agree, all the transactions are executed even these days in nano seconds, so if you can figure a way to consistently get in on the action early, you'd have had your fill before others in H1 or H4 join the train or you could scale out and ride the trend.

Some scalpers use the M15 some even H4, so M1 trading is not just merely scalping.

--- 帖子 #35 ---
Morning Rooi, I have a quick scan of the overnight action since London close yesterday and note any hi/lo's. If there's any continuing direction from yesterday I'll be aware of it. I don't as a rule pay too much heed to the asian activity because when London/europe comes in they will have their own agenda and will dictate procedure from then. One thing I do watch for is the price positioning that takes place in the asian session by the big banks/institutions, hedgies etc where they often position price according to their imminent option expiries. If they're large expiries and PA is close to strike then I won't expect price to move much from that barrier, unless there is relevant and surprise news.

All that considered I watch GU, EJ, EU, UJ, AU but the first 3 mainly. My personal preference is GU but I'll take the first signal I see and today EU & GU weren't showing much so took the EJ off the 6.45 signal and exited at -3 on one of its reversals. Since then not much has happened on EJ so sat on my hands for a while.

While writing this I've entered EU short off the 8.41 signal, I've closed half for +8 so now in profit +1 and letting the other half run on a BE sl. Nearly out there, will go now and watch this trade, speak later. Well, that's that then, did exit on BE.

--- 帖子 #37 ---
Hi Rooi, yes I do look at continuation trades and this is one area where I really like genesis (rather than bago). If you're taken out of a G1m trade after banking tp1 and possibly 2 then the original G signal will have broken down. So if the direction is going to continue, all you need to do is watch for the signal to re-establish itself and consider whether and how to use the next G1m signal. Depending on the setup it could then be a continuation trade or a new entry. For me, at present I'm using only one TP during december so any re-entry would normally be a new trade unless I reduce the stake size.

rgds, strada.

This chart is what I prefer to use - candlesticks and William Bauer's Tick Volume Index - so not another rehash of PA, but an analysys of the volume, tick by tick.  Its main use for me is divergence and as you can see, the second push down had TVI higher - so +ve divergence and coupled with the red high volume in that red hammer that was the low tells me to bank......OK, I was already out, but that's because I'm an early banker in Frankies Hour.....

That would depend on whose thread I was posting in! - Sonic prefered the 34 ema and Genesis works with the 5 / 25 ema, so it would be say the1m 25 ema then 5x 25 = 125 ema for a Genesis post and 34 / 170 in a Sonic post

--- 帖子 #111 ---
Hello Anthm, how are you?

Thanks Rooi. Recovery mode I'll sometimes reduce stake size, but I keep the trade exit plan totally flexible. if I'm down say -20 and I have a trade sitting at +7/8 with 3 TP's I'll close all 3 and finish with +1 for the day. If however I'm down a lot  more than that then I'd probably take "best" profit on TP1&2 and let 3 run but on a very tight leash, not allowing any gains to go too far back. Last resort Ill scalp it and tend to use naked charts for that or maybe C4.

I think it was Marty who said on the other thread that we have to be happy with what the market wants to give us (words to that effect) and I've always held to that. Even when I traded with a daily target I never presumed to expect it every/any day, that would be tantamount to thinking I was better than the market. And this is why I often exit trades earlier rather than later, I don't see the point in pushing a trade too hard in the belief that it may be a runner. Using the exits available on either system means you bank profits and if it is a runner then the opportunity will present itself to re-enter and take more from the move, but the important thing is that you already have profit in the bank. On the other thread I constantly see good trades with good profit going back to BE. If I allowed that to happen, I think I'd be looking for another business opportunity. Using 2 TP like you do, you'll avoid most of that fortunately. Hope some of this helps, regards, strada.

--- 帖子 #132 ---
This is the difficult balancing part of the strategy Rooi. Either taking the early smaller profit on TP1 or aiming for a higher one. Pros and cons for either. Smaller tp1 means putting your trade into profit early but there will be occasions when it will be too early if price comes back and closes the rest of your trade at BE and then turns and moves on in the direction of your trade and you are left sitting on your hands (albeit with a profit but possibly a small one in relation to the size of the move). The higher TP1 will more often cause you to go back into the minuses, and then you're thinking you could have had +8 or 10 etc. So a difficult quandary. For what it's worth, especially trading 1min charts, I most definitely prefer the lower and more realistic TP1. Although I'm fairly aggressive on entries I like to be as stress free as possible and the lower TP1 helps greatly in that regard. If there's a decent move on then I'll let TP2 take care of that.

Just my 0.02c worth, it's a good idea to watch how often both scenarios play out, I'll be doing it cause the old rules from bago may not entirely suit G1m.

regards, strada.

--- 帖子 #214 ---
Hi Kobiet,

BRN stands for Big Round Number. So , for instance, just looking at the Euro Jpy at the moment price is at 141.68. the next highest BRN is 142.0 to the upside and to the downside its 141.0

Some will argue and say the nest BRN to the downside is 141.50 but for me that would be too much filtering.

Hope that helps

Regards

Anthm

--- 帖子 #224 ---
A few things broken but nothing that can't be replaced

The Yen and the Kiwi are vastly different currencies and different economies. Just very briefly, when the Japan earthquake hit, the Yen gained strength because a lot of Yen is 'overseas', and that money would head back to Japan for rebuilding etc etc. This repatriation of the Yen to Japan is what caused the rise in the Yen value. Same happened in the kobe earthquake several years earlier.

With NZ's small economy, which relies mainly on farming exports etc, there is no money overseas to 'repatriate.' So the billions that it cost for the rebuild has to be borrowed, adding to the deficit. This is bad for the currency in the short term, but as the rebuild gets under way, employment is provided and infrastructure etc etc etc is modernised, which helps with consumer optimism blah, blah.....so the Kiwi rises in the mid to long term.....but suffers a short term immediate hit.   <---- in a nutshell!

--- 帖子 #322 ---
Discipline yourself to take clean setups. The odds are in your favor.  At th end of the week go back and look at your clean setups.  What did they do, how did they perform? Then look at the "more risky" setups that you are happy with  (although I do not believe that).  How did they perform.

The goal is to take the setups when the odds are in your favor. If you have fewer of them so be it, stop trading out of boredom...focus on clean setups ONLY for two weeks. Once you recognize the effect they have on your account, you can increase your risk per trade.  It does not take long to build an account.  If you don't develop discipline, you will slowly slip under water until you drown.

I have a strong feeling it is not the clean setups that are the problem.

--- 帖子 #323 ---
Death by a  thousand cuts. Limit yourself to perhaps 1 or 2 trades per session....I don't know if you do this full time or not. Fear of missing out etc......the point of this is not to beat oneself up for missing trades...it is to make money.  Trade the first two hours of whatever session is available. If there are numbers during that time, wait for the market to settle, cycle, and look for a fresh setup.

I don;t want to take up too much of this thread with this discussion.  Feel free to PM me any time.

--- 帖子 #387 ---
Whilst waiting for LO - I have had some questions about the ribbon.....first, its a very visual trend indicator - the wider the red / green band, the stronger the trend, so do NOT trade against it!.

Second, it will always be slow at the turns, so I just watch the fast EMA -( now the 25EMA and my 60 is now also an EMA) and allow myself to enter as soon as price crosses it AND the line changes colour....I hope this helps.....

--- 帖子 #393 ---
This morning I was monitoring 1m GU and UJ as well as the 5m charts.....the 1m allowed me to take this trade..

Ref. the Ultra Stochs, for me its their levels that are most important.  M15 < 20 = Sell Zone, so only sell.  M15 > 80 = Buy Zone, only Buy.  Above the 50 Level, Buy with care.  Below 50, sell with care.  Then use the cycles of the 5m stoch - together with the matrix and 25 ema - to time entries.

That's the simple version - monitoring higher TFs etc is also part of the process.....

--- 帖子 #395 ---
Here we go Ill try and explain as best possible

Lines number in chart

#1 Your stock crosses but flat on top of each other (leaving a bit of doubt)

My stock is blue and I have no doubt

Normal stoc is starting to open and it tells you,you can go long

color stoch is blue and so is long.

#2 Then lines up the matrix for me as I dont have the bottom two bars then siganl bar high gets taken out and I can enter if I want

#3 Normal stoch line sits on top of each other.

color stoch is red so no doubt for me

Also the matrix lines up so I can draw a sinal line but price does not break it so no entry

#4 Normal one starts to open but Im not too happy because they are sitting on top of each other really.

color stoch blue so now Im waiting for the matrix

#5 matrix lines up

#6 breaks the signal line and Im long and no problem with my stoch to figure out what is is doing as I just glance down to see the color as I need to focus on the PA

#7 & 8 leaves the normal stoch lines on each other while I just have glance and chech the color on the color changing stoch

#9 is easy as the color stoch is red then matrix turns red  followed by the signal line(the high or low of the signal candel) gets taken out and im short.

All in all it leaves much less to for me to think about because there is plenty to take into considereation already I just want to check the color of the stock not try to figure out which side the line is and if it opening or closing.Is this the only way to do it?Certainly not.Look at Strada's charts he has the old school ultraStoch.

Down to how and what you need to find out from the indicator.

Hope this help

--- 帖子 #476 ---
Hi - first as I mistakenly installed my MT4 the old way and in the Program Files, this version does not allow me to post templetes.  My BBs are Period 30 and MA Type 1.  Please ask if you need any further info.

Second - my apologies for not explaining my use of the Stochs correctly - I was hurrying to reply to a PM for a newer trader and did not explain myself well.

So the OB/ OS zones are for continuations and whilst the M15 remains there, I am only trading in that direction.

Once the M15 moves out of a zone and has changed to the opposite colour above (below) the 50 take a cautious trade in the new direction.  When the 50 has been broken and held in the new direction take a normal trade in the new direction - or add to the existing trade.  All this is when / if allowed by the matrix and 25 ema.

This remains work in progress and also my trades are agressive and for advanced, experienced traders at their own risk.

My apologies for any missunderstanding

Regards

Islander

PS Please also remember that the Ultra stochs are only 1 out of half a dozen inputs for an entry and that for a Yen Cross I am also considering the same inputs for its two constituent pairs....I have stated this many times....

--- 帖子 #493 ---
EJ and GJ started out - I believe I am correct - as synthetic crosses.....now they are heavily traded and have a life of their own and often influence their "parents"

To get the value of the cross multiply the values of its two base pairs.......so EurUsd x UsdJpy = EurJpy and Gbp x UsdJpy = GbpJpy.   I'm certain you can work out the remainder of the maths....

PS Just banked a few from a long short legged euro as I didnt see any nice long legged yens about....

--- 帖子 #546 ---
So guess you are not going to reply but what I wanted to make you think about was that you asked a question about the MTF Stoch but dropped the line on the

MA ribbon cross. Remember what every type of indicator is for and what there strength and weaknesses are.

Your first line would have been a very nice entry based on the MA ribbon.The MA ribbon works well when you go from a low range Asia session into the London volume as it very responsive at that time of the morning as your candles start to get bigger and so the way the MAs are calculated works nicely in that situation.

Look at the way Islander uses the Bollinger  Bands to show him when the candle are condensing and consolidating and then he uses the ribbon and other indicators once the PA starts getting bigger.

Just my 2 cents as I use to use the ribbon and enjoyed it although you have to know how and when it works best.

Hope it makes it a bit clearer just thought I want to point it out

GL and happy piping

Rooi

--- 帖子 #552 ---
Today i want to share my one of the favourite method of scalping with charts. Use Genesis trading method. Wait for the price to move to OB or OS area. Now in the chart you can see that price is in OS area and there are two lines. Ignore First line which is first crossing in upward direction. But if price go down and there is crossing in downward direction then place one short position and you can get some pips for sure.

Regards

--- 帖子 #575 ---
For monitoring multiple charts - especially when some / most of them are minimised - I use alerts , preferably those which pop-up with the name of the contract and also sound an alert.

Whilst the G Matrix has such an alert, I prefer the flexibility of the ASCTrend indicator which has three variables via its on screen properties box. Also, by putting arrows on the chart, we can look back at the signals generated and research variable inputs.

The standard version version in the "Additional Indicators for the GM trading system" thread only put the arrows on the chart and Marty Fish first modified that version in April 2013 to give a basic alert and now Xaphod has patiently spent time with me to get to the attached version which shows the arrows and has the option of a pop-up and audio alert. Again, many thanks Xaphod

IF - as I do - you like a more personalised sound alert, then I have also attached some sound files - just copy any or all into your MT4 "sounds" folder - no need to reboot. Then on the top screen tool bar go to Tools>Options>Events and change the Alert line to say "air_raid.wav" Do NOT forget to add the .wav to the name of the sound file! .....you may find some of the sounds rather "too much" - that's why I included so many!!

Change the "Risk" factor to give YOU the signals that best suite your trading....scalpers will need a small number, swing traders a higher etc....

Good trading and many green pips

--- 帖子 #664 ---
We should not be doing it in this way as program files folder is for "windows" to use and has a different security level/setting and so you do not want stuff that gets updated regular in that folder if there is any contamination in what you upgrade that then there is a problem according to my knowledge.Also im sure that the program files folder is the the intial destination folder when you download the installer for mt4 so there should not be to big a problem there IMHO

I have  4 different mt4s installed in my program file folder and just one outside of it.

Best to do is copy your existing mt4 folder onto a removable usb stick and keep it there for now.

I will do the same and have then we can always just upload it again if there is a problem even if for now we just use the old build to give us the indicators and the new build to take the trades.

Im sure there will be a better solution in no time BUT we just need to be able to keep ourselfs trading for now.

--- 帖子 #687 ---
Hi Jeffray, the most effective way to check the accuracy of the various stochs is to line up your chart above alongside a basic 5m chart with standard stoch set at same values (11,3,3) and compare the real-time values. Likewise with 15min. I can't speak for the colour ultra as I use only the standard ultra, but I can assure you that the standard version is spot on realtime. Don't take my word for it though, have a look at it for yourself, that way you'll have much more confidence in what you use.

hope you get your charts how you like them, all the best, strada.

--- 帖子 #690 ---
There may be, but what to do is if you have not accepted one click on your MT4,is to reduce the volume or lot size before closing the trade that way part of the trade is still on.

If you have accepted one click, you may want to uninstall your platform and re-install it then when you place a trade and are prompted for one click simply decline so you can be taking advantage of scaling out of your trades.

Please bear in mind the Build 600 implications on uninstalling and re-installing your MT4 platform

--- 帖子 #694 ---
Greetings. I feel the urge to post. I have been absent for a little while so a bit homeless but you guys seem to be doing similar things to me so thought I would drop in. Hope thats ok. I will share my current set up. Its a good discipline to be able to write it down and I have not done so yet. Flavours of Genesis, Three Dragons, Sonic as well as influences recently from Islander, Dmitry fx and Dr Phoenix and a few others all mixed and extracted as I like. Any way its what I am using now so there.

I work off three timeframes. M15, M5 and M1. Each uses MTF stochs (Utra Stochastics - all credits to its creators) each with three stochs, volume (Sonic) and RSI with MA's. Oh and three dragons (which are a variety of MA's and one ribbon MA). Fairly early days for this set up as I have not been trading lately. Here was a trade from this morning, prior to the news. There were better examples but this is one I took before quiting for the day.

Looking at M15 first:

Attached Image (click to enlarge)

The daily stoch was hugging the lower reaches and the 4H stoch was showing signs of weakening as well as price being below the MA's - reasonable probability of a down move.

Moving to M5:

Attached Image (click to enlarge)

Whilst the stoch had a small up move it was in an overall downtrend and critically PA failed to make new highs. Also volume was more at the top (but very thin). The H4 stoch and M15 stoch turned down from high positions, but more importantly there was a 3 dragons (all MA's sloping down) which broke from a touch of the MA ribbon I use. H1 stoch was rising so this was only ever going to be a small run.

And finally M1:

Attachment
Attached Image (click to enlarge)

The key was the turning of the three stochs at the higher side of the range. The green H1 stoch was an issue on this one and I will try to post a better example where it is a clear cut case but there was enough evidence here for me to short. The other factors were the volume on the up bar that then failed, the three dragons, a convincing break on the RSI and finally volume on some nice down bars. I held this until shortly before the news when I decided to close 90% of my position as I had made my numbers for the day and did not fancy the action - volume before the news was enough to send my finger to the close button. My entry and exit were not perfect but I got 19 pips here as well as similar trades on gold and GBP/AUD which gave me enough for the day.

--- 帖子 #724 ---
Thing with partial profit taking it that with all things in trading the general idea is the same but people interpret it differently and I personally have changed the way I think about it a couple of times and will in future most probably.

You said " (tried this morning too) but it just dont work"

What do you mean by that? did the trade not work,did the 2nd TP get taken out for BE.Why would you say it didnt work.If you look at strada's trades for example he gets stopped out for BE on the second TP for 0 or maybe 1 pip and if you ask him if he the trade was successful he will say yes because his TP 1 was hit for +6 and his TP2 was taken out for BE and so protected the profit that he had.He would have liked the market to go further in his direction but he will be ok with being taken out at BE

So when deciding your exit strategy then you must look at why you pick the "split" of the TP's and then look at the targets you wan to hit and how often the SL gets hit for BE.Look at my trades this morning.My TP1 get hit for +3 and then I set my SL to -3 and so will get taken out for BE(minus commissions) and will be happy with that because the TP1 is reducing my risk on the second TP that I look for extended targets and give it a bit of room.Most people will say that way of looking at it is wrong but im happy with(for now).Each to their own

These are just some of the things you can consider when deciding.Hope this helps and if you edit your original reply and quote one of Strada's post Im sure he will take the time to answer.

Hope this helps.

Rooi

--- 帖子 #738 ---
If the volume button does not work t means you must have accepted the one click tool terms and conditions,

For you to be able to scale out of your positions using the volume button after you have accepted one click, you will have to click on tools on your broker platform click on Options, select Trade from the menu box and uncheck One Click trading to get you back to default settings.

--- 帖子 #742 ---
Huskyboy you will find that a lot on here that will use MT4 for analysis but wont necessarily use it for their trade execution. Further to this and in actual fact they may use MT4 of one broker for analysis and be using a completely different broker for trade execution. All brokers platforms are slightly different and some are extremely easy for closing partial positions.

This is why also some cant show their trade history as the round circles with triangles in with a line extending to each, that shows precisely where entry and exit took place. Roois charts are a good example of what I am talking about as he places his trades with his MT4 broker. He can therefore show the triangles with line attached.

Cheers

anthm

--- 帖子 #797 ---
Hi strada.

Here is what I have done so far.

Go to any mt4 downloader or broker site  and download the new build and a new "instance" of mt4 and save it in my documents folder on the C drive and then install the new Zip folder files in the "new" mt4 instance and then update you charts and see if it works.That way you will forever have your old build on you computer working well as long as you leave it in you "programs files" folder they can not change it.You might in future not be able to trade from it but that wont be a problem for you.

So you have two mt4s.The old build in you program files and the new one you downloaded to your C drive in documents.Its a bit of work but will give you an insurance policy and peace of mind while everything is ironed out with indicators and platform etc.

For now im still able to trade of my old build and will update my new "instance" of mt4 with the new indies and updates and get it to work properly.Then I dont have to use the old build BUT I will always have it for backup.Send me a PM if I must explain a bit better or in detail.

I have to run.See you guys a bit later

Rooi

--- 帖子 #833 ---
Morning Anthm

I just use the trend line tool (it should be on a task bar or the insert menu)

The most basic way and most important yellow line that I draw and look at is the double top/bottom ( DT / DB )

The DT/DB works well because if you think why it forms will give you a great view of the market.A DT / DB only means that the traders that move the market have decided to move the market in a different direction and so giving a top/bottom.

Other traders that come into the market that were trading in the other direction will see this move as a retracement and push it back again to the original high or low where the Big Boys will stop it and try again.

I want to try and identify that second stop and reverse because that is the pattern I love the most because of what it means is happening in the market and there is usually a very small SL on those types of DT and DB because if that top or bottom breaks then that means the Big Traders cannot for the moment defend that level.

Please bear in mind this is how I see it and it could very well be a monkey in space causes Double Top or Double bottoms and I dont want 200 people posting that I am wrong and they are right.This is just how I see it.

It takes a little time to get use to looking for it but it really helps

Look at the chart

1 - market makes a new high and stops at the round number and starts to drop

2 bulls think is a retrace and go for the high again

3 the double top forms and they have now capped price ( Genesis should line anywhere in the first 2-5 red candles)

4 the bulls make a double bottom and you can take your first TP of here and SL to BE

5 Big Boys and now retail all start jumping in and makes a push for 6

6 We make a Lower Low and try again

7 Makes a lower Double top and they push on.

8 & 9 Can happen for many reasons normally on the 5 min TF traders trading the 382 fib retracement of the move or what ever really.Hopefully you have stronger mind than me and you have not dumped TP2 yet and you can now take a nice extend target

10 Fails to make a double top

11 Fails to make a double bottom

12 Makes a double bottom we can try again .

It might not always be this clear but it is always there.The moves cant happen without patters and the DT / DB is the best and easiest in my opinion.

All vertical yellow lines are entries subject to GEN lining up

The HA candles help to see the top and bottom better because of the color change

Hope this help to show how or when I draw it.

Rooi

--- 帖子 #950 ---
I changed to just the TVI_V2 as I had noticed that the top line of the matrix was usually the first to change colour by 1 or 2 bars before the others and as I am trading the 1m charts this is important.  Also, the actual TVI gives 3 signals - its change of colour, its cross of the zero line and divergence at turns - so for the advanced trader, more info IMO than the matrix.....remember that I still have 5m & 15m charts open, but I usually just post the 1m....

“Why not trade the higher TFs. Firstly, which TFs to trade is not only personal preference, but is also dictated by the time a trader has available to actually trade.

I live in Spain and thus in THE best TZ for trading the European Session which has 4 major market closes and 3 major market opens. This allows me to trade the shorter TFs and take advantage of the smaller Intra Day Swings which offer between 150% and 200% more pips than the Average Daily Range. I also prefer the action offered by the lower TFs. “

There's a lot more to read in the post...

http://www.forexfactory.com/showthre...80#post7255080

And reading some of his slightly earlier posts you see his multiscreen (including m15) chart setup (in fact he posted one of these in the last couple of days), would find out he his is still tweaking method (and what has changed in recent times) and that he updates his H4 charts BY HAND...[Edit: and that his cloud is an MA Ribbon] it's amazing what you learn with a little research

--- 帖子 #983 ---
It is mostly aesthetics  Being able to quickly look at a chart and match the ultra stoch with the binary direction of the tape. I like the visual contrast.

I've also modified the tape on one of my charts so that it changes colour based on above or below 50 (with a higher stoch), but I'm not using it at the moment since I'm trying to focus shorter-term to reduce my risk.

Thanks Renaldo, that is the M30 10SMA drawn on the M1 chart. I use an indi called 'All MTF MA', it allows you to draw MAs, esp EMAs, from a higher TF on a lower TF properly, and it draws them in steps which is pleasing to my eye for some weird reason!

It just gives me trend, I try to trade long above it and short below, but will trade against it with good reason eg a divergence

--- 帖子 #1061 ---
Since I am not allowed to post on the genesis thread I will include this here.  I hired a programmer to automate Genesis matrix according to Xaphods Dash which includes 4 different columns  essentially genesis matrix with 4 different times frames.  At the time I was confident this was going to work but the problem still lies with consolidating markets which I assumed would be filtered out by  a 1 hour 4 hour and daily column.  In order to run this successfully you will still  need to download the necessary indicators from Xaphods thread.  If you have any ideas to make this successful  I can include it in an updated version of the EA but It will still need   to be fully back tested manually prior to investing any more money into an EA that's not fully functional.  I am still unsure if this will  run  on the new mt4 build so please don't ask me anything I am unsure of myself.   These are the rules:

All trades will be based off the Dash indicator which includes 4 time frame columns based on the Matrix.  Entry and Exits will be included below.

1. Column 1 will be the trigger and will enter only when columns 2,3 and 4 is all the same color.  I would like to configure the time frames to my liking.

2. Trade will exit when column 1 turns opposite color.

3. Hard stops, limits and trailing stops will also  be programmed into the ea along with a news filter.

If you have an opportunity I would read RJ's 1 minute PDF file from the genesis thread because its a wealth of information. Honestly price action and chart reading is the key to exiting losers quickly. As for my own analysis the 30 minute stochastic is a key indication of price strength. If the 30 minute doesn't follow thru after entering utilizing my 1 minute chart 5 15 minute stochastic I will exit quickly with a minimal loss. You will notice the 30 minute stochastic didn't have any follow thru (flat) when I entered however the stubborn person I am, I did enter more then once even when the 30 minute didn't agree.

Regarding the EA

Its very difficult to get proper EA that works really well as a lot of trading is "perception" as you know.EA's are mathematical instruments and so must be have a mathematical explainable edge.Very difficult to find IMHO.

Like I said I will have a play about the idea but they tend to be very complex if they are to be successful.A GenMatrix EA is always a good idea as the signals can be very logical.I most probably think that it would be a multiple entry system based on the scaling into swings as the different time frames start to change into the same direction as some algos are written in this format but lets give it some time and we can have a play with it.Feel free to pm me or I will pm you but I have boat loads on my plate as is and will try and have a look at it after London closes tonight.Can promise it will deliver anything as I have yet to see a really really good EA but then again its not something I spend to much time searching for either.I have played around with some of my own ideas as I do think there is a great future in it for someone who can understand it.

--- 帖子 #1120 ---
Go to View>Toolbars and select which of the 4 options you want to display. Then right click on the vertical hashed line on the left side of each selected option and select "Customize" this then allows you to Insert or Remove from the Available list in the left side.......I customise ALL of my tool bars

--- 帖子 #1178 ---
I don't rely on trading as an income. I've been trading forex for 2.5 years and have devoted most of my energy towards it. It has been incredibly challenging and difficult for me - which is something that I had heard when I began trading, but of course didn't think applied to me  Turns out that it did. Previously traded shares, successfully, using financial models (so more fundamental than technical) albeit over longer timeframes (e.g. 6 months). I also used financial models to build index based valuations, with the intent to trade on, but that was a lower priority to forex trading and also somewhat redundant with QE messing up the global markets connection to fundamentals.

In my time with forex (and technical/systemic trading) I've spent maybe 50 hours per week (so 6500 hours?) learning. I'm still learning. My wife has named my charts 'squiggles'. It has been challenging in that I was in an accident a year and a half ago and have experienced pain since then. It does impact on concentration - but then we all have our own problems. In my time learning, I've tried 1000's of different indicators and combinations. LOL just checked and I have 1145 indicators in my MT4 and that exludes those that have been removed. I learned how to code EAs and tried that for a while - even had one which I was certain would be profitable ($1000 -> $10,000,000 in six months with 20% DD on backtest based on a solid strategy) but just couldn't make them work in all environments and gave up on them. I learned how indicator coding worked and have spent a lot of time fiddling with custom alert settings. I guess that could be an 'edge' in that I have very specific parameters that I'm waiting for before I'll even consider a trade. It remains a work in progress - but seems to constantly improve as does my trading.

My goal is to have trading income sufficient to be my prime source of income this year. I know I can do it, my only hurdle is myself and to be consistent. Mistake reduction is my prime strategy at the moment!

Sorry for the spiel. Interested to hear your story and that of anyone else willing to share?

--- 帖子 #1209 ---
Regarding LFH trading simulator: it is not an EA to make trades but a tool to simulate historical price action and to simulate trades through scripts. The backtesting functionality of MT4 uses EAs (strategy tester).

--- 帖子 #1215 ---
While I'm in sharing mode, I thought I'd also share another indicator that I like and have modified for my own purposes.

The indicator is another MTF stochastic that called AllStochastic and I guess is in between Stoch-MTF and !UltraStoch. Additionally it adds many different modes for the signal (%D) moving average type. The author of AllStochastic is IgorAD from Trend Laboratory.

I modified it so that it would change colour when K crosses D and so that it visually looks similar to !UltraStochastic. It is not a replacement to !Ultra (IMO), but from my perspective, it can complement it.

Here is a screenshot.

Attached Image (click to enlarge)

As with most MTF indicators, it will repaint the current bar until it closes. It does work in LFH simulator, but obviously it doesn't take in to account the swings during the time-frame - especially at higher time-frames.

I am an amateur coder, so hopefully there are no problems with it

Attached File(s)   AllStochastics_Auto.ex4

104 KB
|
1,164 downloads

Whilst my idea of monitoring both components of the GbpJpy and EurJpy crosses may seem complicated, its really not difficult.

These are my two monitors, one for the 5m charts and the other for the 1 min charts.

As soon as the 1 min AscTrend fires its pop-up alert and sounds its own special sound alarm I take a close look at the charts make my decision - to enter or not.

If its "not" then I carry on with other things - like reading my book - in summer by my pool

Now I am flat on this research account and finished for this morning.

I never trade with trend because i do not believe that trend is my friend. It could be your friend but not mine.

Here i try my best in short time to give some explanation because i have other job too but i think it will be confusing for you.

On the last chart you have seen that first level is created by indi at 1.3875 but on the other side you need to remember that FOMC reaction is 100 Pips approximately. I think level of 1.3875 has moved down to 60 pips. Once it it is clear for me that new level is stable then i will start placing trades in consolidation area. I can say that i have ability to handle consolidation area rather than trend.

I forgot to add something that if you look at the charts which i have posted earlier, you will find that i have used 1.3900 psychological level which gave me around 65 Pips.

--- 帖子 #1473 ---
Hi Rooi and all, just dropping by to say hello, hope you're well and still enjoying your trading, nice to see the pip gains being made here.

@Islander, your paper charts take me back a bit. Don't know if you were around in the days when that was all we poor retail traders had because the prohibitive expense of charting programmes left us no option. So all plotting done by hand including the calcs for MA's, RSI, MACD, etc. Surprised we had time to determine entries and exits as well (which of course had to be done by phone)!!

Then along came the first computer (with the 5.5" floppy DOS disk). Wow, what an advance that was. Found a graphing programme but still had to manually calculate MA's etc. Then for trendlines and S&R it was elastic bands and string with blue-tac across the front of the screen.

The good old days??? Not on your life!!!!!!!!

@Aahmad29 ~ I like your style of using PA, you clearly have a good understanding of its behaviour with smaller timeframe charts, and especially without the need for using higher tf trends etc. I do likewise, and don't feel the need for such filtering. currently running at losing ratio of less than 20% over all trades taken this year on basic (though aggressive) G1m. Doubt very much any additional filters would improve on that.

--- 帖子 #1479 ---
GM - some time ago I posted about another risk that many traders ignore.......remember these big companies.....Refco and MAN Financial, the biggest in the buisness and both went bust with millions of clients money, so I NEVER put all of my funds with just one broker, nor do I put all of my trading funds there....I keep around half in my own bank and use their gearing / leverage.

So I trade with ~ 30:1 to 50:1 gearing / leverage with similar stops to yours and if price moves back to cross the 25EMA I get out....

--- 帖子 #1501 ---
If you are asking me, then yes, I prefer to trade in the same direction as the 5m arrow, PROVIDED that the 5m 25ema has some slope showing that there is a trend in place.......as you can see from my multi screen posted a couple of days ago, I continually monitor the 5m charts and regularly check the higher TFs for S&R areas, TLs etc.   Waiting for the higher TFs to line up is IMO not necessary for day trading off the 1 min charts.

--- 帖子 #1503 ---
LOL - been there, done that too. When I trade by my rules I have an 80% + win rate.......when I break my rules I have an 80%+ loss rate!

I use this simple Trade Sheet for each entry.......when an ASCTrend Alert pops up the numbers 1 - 8 are the items that require a tick to allow an entry.....

1. Is price in a BB Squeeze? 2. Has the 25 EMA changed colour to agree with the Signal Arrow? 3. Is price within x pips of the 25EMA etc.......you can work out the remainder as I've talked about them often.....or use some of your own....

Total 5 out of 8 allows a trade.......

Morning Rooi and all. The chart may make it look simple today but I can assure you it wasn't. Sometimes I'd stay well clear of this type of terrain, but I'd started, so.............!

Someone will almost certainly tell me I was on the wrong pair today, but I'd started on GU and don't like switching.

It was one of those nip'n'tuck days and the last trade was going to be my last G1m trade before switching to recovery mode, in fact I think I was already in recovery mode mentally but the trade went so well decided to run it as normal.

So I'm sure Islander will agree, days like today are far from simple, it isn't so much about years of experience as it is about a sound trading strategy with well-founded rules and realistic expectations. And this has to include a plan for when you're in a hole. Very, very important, this is probably where most people lose accounts.

--- 帖子 #1545 ---
I just use the coloured volume bars as an alert to look closely at what's happening.  Increasing tick volume is increasing activity and so this tells us to pay attention.

I use this more when price has moved close to "a level" on a chart.....the level may be a sweet spot, a pivot level or a S&R zone and I will often take some profits.   In 1m trading we need to be nimble and banking 10 or so pips does wonders for our moral and account balance

--- 帖子 #1615 ---
This is by far one the of the best most informative post I have ever read on forex factory.  It was written by Hanover one of the biggest contributors referring to a self proclaimed holy grail system FF thread.  I will copy and paste here.

I'm sorry. It looks like my post jinxed your Trade Explorer. After 2 years and 16000 pips, I go ahead and post, and it's now encountered some significant losses. I see that you've changed your first post to "Those looking for holy grail of forex - this is NOT it".

@readers of the Rookie forum:

There's a "this is the holy grail" thread every few months on these forums. I've been a member since 2006, and during that time none of them have lasted more than a few months. People overestimate their own genius: they believe that they've discovered something revolutionary that all the millions who have gone before them, including the most experienced traders and knowledgeable market veterans, have somehow overlooked. They forget that, if a simple "holy grail" grid system existed, that the big banks and institutions could save themselves millions in salaries by dismissing all of their expert analysts, traders, economists and IT gurus, and simply run this holy grail.

Am I being negative? No, because I know that it's very possible to be a profitable forex trader. I know of at least two regular FF contributors who run accounts totalling several million dollars. I have other buddies and acquaintances who are profitable, albeit to a a more modest extent. All of these folk are successful because:Their strategy incorporates a proven edge, one that is grounded in exploiting recurring inefficiencies in price behavior. They accept losses, and exit them quickly (whereas the amateur looks to somehow filter out losing trades, and/or recover from recent losses). They prioritize risk management, by sizing their positions both small (relative to account size) and consistently, allowing both their method and their account to survive unfavorable market conditions, and giving their edge the opportunity to ultimately prevail. They focus on improving their market analysis and trade execution, not their P&L. Profit is the by-product of making good trading decisions; chasing money generally results in poor decisions. They understand and avoid the newbie traps listed here (and no doubt many others, also). They know that it requires significant capitalization to be able to size conservatively, and also make a decent income (whereas newbies "need" something like 100% per month from their $1,000 accounts, and consequently overtrade, and overleverage themselves). Their consistent execution involves discipline; and discipline comes from having confidence in a proven strategy, which comes only from experience, and is grounded in knowledge of how and why markets operate.

Yet none of these professionals would ever talk about their approach as being the "holy grail". That is a term used by newbies, and also by vendors who want to lure newbies into buying their worthless products.

I'm no longer using MT4 or trading FX. Pls don't expect replies to posts.

--- 帖子 #1623 ---
Hi gkawa

I trade only the FO and LO with a target of getting as close to 20 pips as I can without forcing it to much.Like now I have +17 and Im happy with that.No need to cause myself any heart ache by risking profits.

I changed how I trade a great deal in the last four months as I had been spending 10hours a day in front of the charts trying to catch as much as I can and trying to understand everything and every session but at the end of it all I never once made 100pips at the end of the day because I was over trading and really making and losing a lot of pips but my end result would normally be anything from -30 to +30 for the whole day.

I have followed Strada for a long time and he has really been through it all and has a very long history with trading and you can see it in his results.He only maybe has one or two losing days in a year if that, with a target of 30 pips a day but more importantly closer to 600pips a month trading only FO and LO.So not chasing  the pips on the bad days but rather making plenty on the good days.Knowing there will be plenty of both.

So when I looked into some of my results I realized that there was no real benefit to trading from London open to London close as I was not making more pips just causing myself a lot of head ache by winning and losing pips the whole day long.Others like Islander might be great at the NY session but it very difficult in my opinion there is always a great deal of news and all sorts happening and after a whole morning of trading I tend to not think my trades through as well as I should.

Getting back to LO.LO has the cleanest move with a lot of volume so there should be a 95 % chance of the move in either the GU or EJ as you have the 4 main currencies in that group and they behave very well in the 1min with strong moves and reversals.

So taking a page out of Strada's book I now only trade 3 hours in the morning and give it my full attention.Still working on making my 20pips a day but as long as I dont have down days then I am slowly growing my account consistently without violent swings.Your risk % can also increase as one becomes very consistent and knowing that you have very few down day

I now have much less head ache in the afternoon and plenty of time to spend doing my other home based job and working on my other venture.

Its much better in my opinion to trade/scalp the cream of the day.The market is just too vast to to be trading the whole time.

Three hours is plenty and you can always do some swing trading or investing like I am doing as well if you like myself , feel the need to always have money in the market

Sorry for the long winded explanation but that's why I only trade FO and LO

All the best

Rooi

--- 帖子 #1633 ---
Hi Kobiet, No, I don't look at 5min or any HTF before trade entry.

This may not find much agreement with most, that doesn't make anyone right or wrong, it just means we're different!

For me, trading 1min is all about 1min charts, nothing less, nothing more, I get all the info I need from that 1 chart. I know for a fact that if I start trying to predetermine direction using HTF charts or indies I will then have bias, I will then hesitate, over-analyse, double/triple check and end up missing perfectly good trades.

But it goes a lot deeper than that. Before switching to G1m I obviously did a lot of research and testing, I had in fact been working with it on the sidelines almost since the genesis inception but using 1min charts, so I developed quite an affinity with it. What I did know was that the method yielded consistent profitable results just as a stand-alone system without any of the additional filters (including some that RJ used) but using my own well established MM.

So when you know that a method is going to give these results, it isn't difficult to run with it and take the inevitable losses in the stride, although they have to be sensibly managed with a decent plan. On this basis I'm not interested in looking for ways to filter out losing trades, it's a waste of time because I know I'll fiilter out more good trades than the bad ones.
I would much rather be in a signalled losing trade than out of a signalled winning trade.

Going a bit deeper, there then has to be a suitable trading plan to capitalise. I used to use 3 TP's before, then Rooi came up with the idea of using 2 and he made it work quite well so I checked it out and followed his example, that has proved extremely beneficial. My targets are relatively low these days because I can't maintain the same levels of concentration any more so smaller targets, higher value pips, I really need to concentrate for that short session each morning and therefore have to keep it all as simple as possible. That means no HTF or additional charts/indies.

Long winded I know but maybe it helps. However please remember, if others do it differently, that doesn't make it wrong, just different.

regards, strada.

--- 帖子 #1640 ---
Hi Islander, apart from any major S&R on the other charts I'll be mindful of any levels prominent from asian session or persisting from previous day but I don't normally put them on the chart, partly due the aesthetics but more importantly they won't have too much influence on entries unless there has been very, very recent weakness at the barriers. I will occasionally use them for exits if PA stalls or fails several attempts to break. After 6am (Europe) & 7am (UK) when the forex desks are getting into full swing I don't think much of the overnight activity plays that much part in proceedings, europe and more so London will have their own agenda and they will determine the way forward so very often overnight levels get swept aside.

Of course there are times when I forget these levels and then afterwards wonder why price got stuck!!! I know what the solution is but like you suggested I prefer not to have the lines on the chart.

regards, strada.

Hi i know that many traders get confused with my trades because trades are not totally depends on indicators. I am testing one trading system here in FF in trading Journals with my own settings. When price hit lower band and there is cross up in BH-Ergodic

Rule for Short Entry:

When price hit upper band and there is cross down in BH-Ergodic

If you are monitoring 12 contracts, many of these will be crosses and thus have similar movements to their base pairs.

As this thread is mainly about the European Session, the main base pairs are EurUsd, GbpUsd, UsdChf, UsdJpy and possibly AudUsd and  their assosciated crosses - EurJpy, GbpJpy EurAud etc - these are the most active majors during this session.

Like Rooi, I restrict my trading mainly to GbpUsd and EurJpy and for some excitement, occasionally UsdTry...

The PA formation will have many names but I learnt it as a failure to return pattern meaning it tested the High of the day and tried to test it again but could not even get back up to test it never mind break it so the path of least resistance it down

--- 帖子 #1663 ---
i do not trade chf, as very highly correlated to EUR. I have one screen for base pairs, EU and GU, one for yen and crosses, one for commodities vs USD. The other I use for any crosses that are moving strongly via a strength meter. It is amazing how many times the synthetic is moving the most.....I.e EN etc. When the arrow alert triggers, I look at the appropriate screen and if the signal is valid I fire away.

--- 帖子 #1777 ---
been working on my charts for a while. It seems i am constantly working on it . But for now i decided i will stay with these and its very close too all the other charts posted here.

My rules are, wait for the Arrow, stoch 5 needs to cross the 40/60 line, stochs 5 and 15 needs to have the same color and have to come out off the OB/OS area, direction has to be confirmed by the EMA 14<>EMA 47, MACD needs to cross its 0-line, there can be a divergence (but doesn't have to be) and confirmation by the matrix m1 and ASCT trend.

Suggestions are welcome. Hopefully i can get some pips IF i ever find time to trade. Wont be next week i guess

The difference is that you can't eat or buy a car with pips.

What is the worth of every pip, how much has your account grown today. If you have a small risk/SL then for the same % risk every pip is worth a lot more than when you have a large SL. With a 10 pip SL your pips could be worth 5 times as much as Aahmads pips.

--- 帖子 #1921 ---
[quote=Jeffray;7431605]{quote} Islander, one simple question  How do you know ehen you have to enter in such a FO/LO breakout move. It is always fascination seeing you trading!  Is it your gut Feeling which is telling you "enter now" or is it based on some indications?[/quote

If you read my posts over the past say three months you will see where I have shown charts with several additional indicators that help any trader to see potential entries - the ASCTrend with alarm and the Bands indicator are two that should help. Once price is in a BB pinch and an alert arrow shows up then look carefully at the chart......again, I have explained several times what I use to actually trigger my entry.

We know that the European Session starts to get active around FO, so by then I have already been looking at my charts for 15 / 20 minutes, analysing the overnight action, updating any S&R levels, short term TLs, HLs or LHs etc, looking for any clues as to what might happen and which charts are showing the most potential - again, I have pages of hand written data showing timing, potential swings etc during this period so this helps - its basic research and hard work, building up your own knowledge base - then trading becomes just a bit easier!

Good luck

--- 帖子 #1994 ---
Hi Rooi, yes very often bago will produce signals at the same time as G1m, but what I found (and one of the reasons I switched to G1m) was that G1m often didn't signal trades that bago did and kept me out of many losing bago trades.

The 2 methods are similar in that they are set up to signal turns in the market so they will often mirror each other.

Re the RSI, I don't pay particular attention to it but as you know I keep bago charts alongside G1m, mainly for pricing entries/exits but also for levels and so on. I do use bago sometimes for exits when convenient, but not much else.

I'm not selective with G1m, have my rules and if signal fits then I go with it. As you say G1m definitely is better than bago during ranging.

Bago and G1m don't always line up simultaneously but they'll normally signal within a couple of bars of each other.

25MA or RSI, they're both serving much the same function, giving us confirmation, so whatever we're most comfortable we'll tend to go with. One point I'll make on "confirmation". I often see people going to extreme lengths looking for all sorts of confirmation for an entry and a line has to be drawn here because the more confirmation people want the more profitable trades they're going to miss out on. They may miss some losing trades but I'll bet they spend a lot of time sitting on their hands totally frustrated wishing they'd made the entry instead of looking for more "confirmation". If we do our homework and verify that a method is profitable then we trade it, we use the valid signals unless there is a very obvious reason not to (red news imminent etc), no ifs or buts. Then we manage our trade within our rules.

Hence ~ I'd rather be in a signaled losing trade than be out of a signaled winning trade.

Hope some of this is of some help, cheers strada.

--- 帖子 #2000 ---
When price is rangebound like now, and you're presented with a signal, for instance the 8am bar on EJ I would have started off with a SL below the 7.53 bar (big SL for me!!).

This is the London open so there may well be enough momentum to push this through, then we'll see if it's london stop hunting or pushing higher.

I would have waited for 1pip improvement before entry.

Seeing the failure to break the number I'd be looking for an improved SL or perhaps an exit, cause if London open can't push this through then it's likely a non-event. The 8.06 low would have given me a bettter SL (with a 1 pip buffer).

It was touched on the 8.14 bar then another attempt at the number.

Another failed attempt, I'd be looking to reduce my exposure or a full exit possibly at BE.

8.26 bar a total disintegration of previous signal and presentation of new short signal. If still in trade would definitely be out now with small loss.

The bars between 8.26 and 8.39 formed a nice ledge so was price gearing up for another go at the number or the other way in line with the latest signal. Given the failure to break so many times I would now be considering short again and may have entered on the break below that ledge. Can't be sure on that, easy to see in hindsight.

Main thing here is that 1min charts provide alot of good information so our losses need never be too high.

regards, strada.

Of course it can go the other way, we just have to be ready for that and have our exit plan worked out.

The exits. well, bouncing around the number and not far off my target, it's the "bird in the hand.........."

And yes, I'm done for the day too close to target to risk any of it, not been a bad week, short of target on that but won't be losing any sleep.

It was nice to see your TP1 for 6, better than 2/3, yes?

regards, strada.

--- 帖子 #2081 ---
Ok heres a trade I am still in from this morning took 7.2 pips from first push now at BE and holding for bigger run, bit hopeful I guess after a good run, but you never know???

Indicator top left shows top trending pairs on 1 min and 5 min it uses the slope of a moving average.  I use 100lwma for 1 min chart. It shows the steepest sloping ma so shows the top 8 trenders as I see it.

I like to find the strongest trending pairs then trade those in that direction eg pullbacks or breakouts(now i've read your thread).  Levels I like to trade break and retest on are. 200sma 25 levels Daily pivots Yesterdays high,low and close price. (yellow lines on my chart) If you look on attached chart theres a couple of prime examples of B&R 141.75 level also yesterdays close very adjacent to it, 200 sma (blue ma).

Very basically I identify a strong trending pair from top 8 trenders then wait for a break and retest of above levels.  Simple really.

--- 帖子 #2095 ---
Hi Clive

Really just depends on the type of news.

Euro opens have there big news but nothing like unemployment number or rate decisions etc that can really whip up and down by 50pip in my opinion.

That being said.Unless Im in a decent position with a SL at BE and a bit of a buffer between current price and the BE price I will never hold a trade or get into a new trade 10 min before new news

I will take a trade 30 seconds after or even closer if the chart gives the signal-many time we move of the high of the day or other nice setups just after news.I dont trade the news or even the reaction but dont mind a decent signal with a decent well placed SL after the news

As for the currency pair I trade,I use Strada's approach of looking at the overnight action and range of either EJ or GU and also take into consideration how the pairs have been behaving recently and 99.9% of the time I will stick to the pair I start trading for the morning

But like you said everyone is different

--- 帖子 #2116 ---
Hi All

This thread is really warming up lovely some great stuff here for sure, hopefully all us 1 minute traders can help each other become better traders.

Anyway found my top 8 trender indy from the platform so here it is.

Attached File(s)   #Top 8 Trenders Indicator.ex4

23 KB
|
1,767 downloads

But before I go any further must give credit to the creator of this indy who worked with me to put this together, Hugh Briss, otherwise known as Ted to his close friends. He is a great guy and coder so if you have any ideas you want coding have a chat with him. I'm sure for the right price he will help you out. Thanks Ted great job.

Oh and he has written a book about trading too, smart guy, heres a link to his book. http://www.amazon.com/Swing-Trading-...nd+stochastics

I will endeavour to explain how it works and the best way I've found to use it but I will say it could be used in numerous ways so heres my ideas.

Basically it measures the steepness of a moving average (you can choose which one) then ranks them in order of steepness so the steepest is at the top. The theory is that the fastest moving pairs, trending the most, will have the steepest sloping MA. We monitor 2 timeframes so you can monitor the timeframe above the one you trade. This is useful for a couple of reasons you can either trade the pair when it comes to the top on both or another way I use it is when the same pair is top in both but opposite colours eg going in opposite directions which means a reversal is imminent.

The whole point of following steep sloping MA's is that when you trade with the trend not only will the momentum carry you to profit quicker but also the momentum indicators work really well giving you a higher strike rate. The GBPUSD daily chart below,for instance, gave you 8 winning entries out of 10.

Attached Image (click to enlarge)

So how does it help? Well first of all look at the top 8 trenders in the daily column and use it as your first filter, go down the list checking out the charts until you see one you like the look of. I liked the look of the gbpusd daily chart(see attached), the red MA is a 100lwma which is the MA used in this example, as you can see GBPUSD is 3rd in our table of top 8 trenders. Check out the others yourself I think theres 4 of the 8 that look really tradable in my opinion.

Now we have our pair to trade and look for a good entry to join the trend.

I like the look of the 1.6800 level for Monday don't you???

So how do we set up the inputs?? See top 8 trenders settings hrly and daily attachment below.

Attached Image (click to enlarge)

the top 2 inputs are used to space out the table x and y position the indicator on your chart the 5th one is fontsize.

tf1 = timeframe 1 in minutes eg 15 = 15min 60 = hrly 1440 = daily 10,080 = weekly 43,200 = monthly etc

tf2 = timeframe 2 as above

tf1malength = timeframe 1 moving average period

tf1type = 0-simple 2-ema 3-lwma 4-smoothed

tf1maprice = timeframe 1 moving average price applied to 0-close 1-open 2-high 3-low etc

tf1lookback = this is how far you want to look back the moving average to measure the slope. I use a multiple of next timeframe up for 60min I use 24 as 24 hours in a day; for 1 min I use 15 as 15min is next timeframe up. Please try out different periods at your discretion.

tf2 settings are the same as above but just for the higher timeframe.

useatr = this is an interesting one where you can choose to take into account the pairs atr so giving it a volitility filter, without it just the biggest movers, most volitile pairs come to the top. I personally set it to false for lower timeframes like 1 min etc but 1 hr and above I set it to true. But again play around with it yourselves see what siuts you best.

Ok so thats the settings now the difficult part, how best to use it?? Heres some of my ideas:

Straight forward trade the trend using cci for entries.

Look at the chart above and you can see that GBPUSD is in the top 3 so check out the chart and look for a CCI signal back with the trend. I use a 8 CCI as pullbacks in a strong trend can be quite small, I also wait for the CCI to go over -100 level to qualify as an entry. Once cci goes over -100 then wait for first smaller cci candle eg momentum is slowing down and looking to reverse. Place a pending order above the signal candle and see if it gets hit next day, if not and cci candle is smaller than yesterdays then move pending order to next daily candle, continue until trade is hit.

Exit at your discretion or hold until the trend ends. Trail all entries up higher lows until stopped out. Or just grab each momentum move at your discretion.

Heres a 1 minute trade example

Attached Image (click to enlarge)

This time the top 8 trender is set up for 1 minute and 5 minute and looking at 1 min you can see its showing top of the trenders but more importantly you can see why look at the 100lwma (red ma) its sloping down perfectly, I tend to use 14 cci on the lower timeframes but theres a nice signal at 11.03 which is also a break and retest of my 200sma, one of my favourite entries, and away you go!!

Exit again is discretionary but heres a couple of choices for you;

First green Hieken ashi candle trail stop to top.

The next support level in this case the yellow line (yesterdays close)

Exit first TP at either above and hold 2nd half until 100lwma is crossed over.

Reversal setup

This is one of my favourite setups usually occurs mid morning on a London Openwhen price has been racing one way for 100pips or so appearing in the top 8 for most of the morning as say red (going down) it will also be in the top 8 of the 5 min trenders too. Wait for it to appear in the 1 min top 8 trenders as opposite colour to 5 min eg Green, then enter as above theres every chance it will go back 70% of the move down.

London breakout strategy/ post news strategy

London is when a lot of money comes to the table and often causes a breakout in one pair or another. Well what better way than to see which 100lwma is pouring up or down the page 30 mins after the open??? Look at the top 3 trenders and checkout the chart for a good setup , I like break and retests of key levels as discussed before eg. 25 levels, 200sma, yesterdays high,low close or the daily pivot. oh and of course S and R levels.

The same theory can be applied to a high differential news release, wait for 10 mins after the news release for price action  to settle down and a new 1 min trend to setup again which 100lwma is sloping the steepest??? The MA can be changed to say a 20 for an immediate response after news but I find a bit too jumpy for normal trading.

SUMMARY

Basically the top 8 trender can be used on any timeframe to identify the strongest moving pairs on that timeframe. When used on the 1 minute timeframe you will find it chops and changes quite a bit so sometimes use the 5 min as your master and wait for 1 min to agree. The bottom line is its an awesome indicator but thats it, its just an indicator you still have to check the chart out and look for a siutable entry, but trust me once you learn how to use it it can be a great help.

One word of warning sometimes when a pair comes to the top it can have already moved quite away so might be about to reverse, so again use your skills to decide whether that pairs worth trading or not. best time for me is when the 100lwma has just turned up or down after a strong move one way or the other, thats when its the best time to get in and hold.

Well that's me done I'm sure theres all sorts of ways to make use of this indy so good luck and if it helps you become a better trader then don't forget to thank Ted, Hugh Briss, without his coding skills it wouldn't be here.

--- 帖子 #2141 ---
Glad you are enjoying the top 8 trender it can certainly help and I think its a good idea to use the 5 min as the master then look for your favourite entries in the 1 min. Don't forget you can use it on higher timeframes too eg daily as master and trade the hourly.

Just a word of warning don't forget all trends come to an end and usually before its shown in the MA so whenever you look at a top trender make sure its still trending strongly and not looking like its exhausted eg was the last push higher a clear push higher?? Is it pulling back to support etc etc I always say to people don't just trade it because its in the top 8 trenders, still use your analysis skills to confirm the trends still going.

And to answer your question the lookback period is 15 bars but of course you can set it for what you want I just use the next timeframe up for my own use please feel free to experiment.

Hi

Just looked back at this mornings charts and saw a setup that I really like so thought I would share it with you all. Its the London mid morning reversal. When the London boys set us all up for a fall by letting price march one way right into all thier orders waiting to eat us alive.

Thing is by trading the 1 min charts you can sometimes see it happening and jump on board. I watch for 2 things really.

1) A pair to appear in the top 8 trenders one colour say green, going up, then an hour later it appears red, going down.

2) I watch for my 15 min CCI to turnover then take the next 2 or 3 1 min cci signals the same way as per charts below.

It happened on EURAUD this morning and gave us a perfect pullback entry at 10.50 gmt to a 25 level (1.4725)

Its gone down about 75 pips since.

By the way watch out for New York reversing this move, I have a personal theory that London and New York have an agreement that one sells something all morning whilst the others buy it all back in the afternoon, that way they both make bucket loads of money. Seen it happen all too often for it to be a coincidence.

So watch for the reversal back up this afternoon. Just a thought.

As per request by PM I will share entry system that I use.

I use the color change on the matrix together with the bars at the bottoms color change

Once the color change happens there should be a 1 pip improvement of the of the signal bar

Not all entries are going to be profitable and working out the best entries are up to you and how you like to trade

The rest of the info is all in the thread to read and there are plenty of examples.I suggest digesting Strada's charts as that is what I do.

The most important of the system is to make your wins bigger than your losers.There will be plenty of loser but you are able make money by keeping them small.

The vertical lines shows possible trades for today

Hope this helps.

Re stats, I did most of my data collating some time back when I was on 5mins and spent hours every day for months collecting material on every signal on 1min charts, I was sure there was something there but had to prove it's consistency etc. data included time, duration, price entry, biggest drawdown, maximum pip gain etc. From that I proved the reliability using some strategies and abject failure using others. --- 帖子 #2233 ---
Yes, it's galling if you're taken out at BE then the trade develops and leaves you on the sidelines.

BUT, consider the alternatives. If you let price slip through your BE stop how far do you let it go? You may by this stage be already in a signalled reverse move, not only are you losing money, you've denied yourself the opportunity of making profit on the reversal.

Plus preserving your capital in this way is as good as a good trade, it is a "position".

Very often when you're taken out at BE the signal that took you into the trade initially will have broken down. If the move re-establishes itself it's quite likely that a new signal will form giving you the opportunity to re-enter either the full trade or just the TP that exited at BE.

All in all, over the term, I've found it a very beneficial rule, but it still hurts when I'm out and the trade goes on to great profit. Sometimes I do break the rule and allow a little flexibility on those days when I think I'm smarter than the market. Invariably I get a sore backside!!

Strada.

@ Jonnypants ~ daily "target" is around 20 but I'm flexible on that, some days I have to settle for +1, and do my best not to have any losing days. Strict believer in the market will only give what it wants to give, so it's up to me to manage my trades within those parameters.

--- 帖子 #2312 ---
No of course I don't mind, its demo at the moment as experimenting with some new strategies on the 1 min charts, but looking to go live again next week if I get some positive results this week.

Basically I am trying to catch the London breakout trades by taking entries in the strongest trending pair through the London open. My theory is whichever 100 lwma is sloping the steepest then thats where the London money is going so jump on board grab a handful of pips with the first push then hold 2nd TP until the trend finishes.

Well thats the theory, But as I aptly demonstrated this morning and as the chart below shows, even on demo its hard to hold until the trend ends. If I had held I would of been close to 130 pips up (had 2 trades open) and still holding.

Trouble is you have so many trades that don't go and you see all your profit disappear, that when you do catch one its hard to hold it???

Oh well work in progress but when I do go live will start my own thread,rather than post all over yours, and fully intend to post a trade explorer so everyone can see how hard it is. LOL.

I did trade a trend system in the past and I can suggest that you split your trade in 2 positions of 0.05 each = 0.1

Then TP 1 = 8 pips @ 0.5

TP 2 then gets split into 5 X 0.01 lots

For example

TP 2.1 = 10 pips

TP 2.2 = 12 pips

TP 2.3 = 15 pips

TP 2.4 = 20 pips

TP 2.5 = a reversal of the MA's or change of CCI

You will have a lot of BE trades though that is just how it is with trend trading IMHO

All tps are relative to your SL

TP1 should equal your SL at the very least to give you a minimum of 1:1 R:R

BUT , there is plenty to consider as should be relative to the ATR of the pair your trading (plenty of back testing though )

Just my 2 cents and please feel free to ignore it completely.
