--- 帖子 #2318 ---
Hi Clive, hope you don't mind me joining in this discussion, you raise some important points worthy of some open discussion.

Trend is a very large part of many traders' decision making process, and understandably so. However, it doesn't have the same level of importance to everyone. I for one rarely ever use it.

Let me say straight away here, that does not make either of us wrong, it just means we have different perspectives and trading mentalities both of which could be as good (or bad) as each other.

Everyone has to somehow prove that whatever method/strategy they intend to use is going to be profitable. As you said, your winners have to yield more than your losers. So we all achieve our chosen strategies with this common goal. BUT, we all do this differently. Many will do it as you have chosen, ie using trend in the belief that your entries will have a decent probability of profit. As I said earlier there is nothing wrong with that, I have no criticism to make. If you can create a consistent profitable strategy around this criteria and it is working for you, you're comfortable with it, then you've cracked it, you will enjoy profitable trading.

The point to be made here is that "trading with trend" isn't the only way, it isn't exclusive to profitable trading, there will always be numerous ways to trade any good method some of which will be very adaptable and others that may well respond better to trending markets, S&R, Pivots etc.. In much the same way as some will say you can't make profit trading 1min you have to trade daily or 4hour charts etc., it really is up to the individual to find their own comfort level with trading and that will come in as many varieties as there are people. It doesn't run that only one way can be right.

The only "wrong" methods/strategies are those that consistently lose money.

Developing a strategy for consistent profit on 1m t/f isn't easy, it has some very distinct characteristics and behaviour which all has to be factored in. You are clearly working hard to find the optimum strategy for you based on trend, I'm sure you'll succeed with that and I wish you every success with it.

strada.

--- 帖子 #2366 ---
Hi Clive

You are very right about the process of it, if your strategy has an edge you will be able to make nice returns.There is nothing wrong with being aggressive and trading with 10% of your capital per trade. If you have $1000 and trade 1 % of your account at 10 pips stop your risk is $10 so $1 per pip

But if you have a $1000 dollars in your account for trading and you take 10% of the account and put it in a a trading account it is $100 and trade it 10% risk it also works out to $1 per pip but your growth is much faster right, with less risk on your money in the bank but more risk on the amount in trading account using leverage.

Your thinking to yourself I know this Rooi and Im sure you do.

So why are we not all billionaires? Because of the pain it causes us when we lose 10% of the account.

Why does it cause us pain? Because we have not tested our system to the point where we can trust it enough to get us through the doubt of making the next trade.

If one can trade for a year using the same system on the same market and produce a certain outcome and work out the draw down and the different stats about the system and your trading then the sky is the limit but we need that trade setup or system that we can rinse and repeat trades.

I always think a lot of us have it backward we want to risk too much with too little knowledge and then it frustrates us.We could have been building a better system and testing it properly rather than being frustrated by watching an account see-saw up and down.How many years are you planning on trading?I plan on trading till just before I die and so what is 1 or 2 years really when building a system that you know like the back of your hand and can truly leverage to its full potential.

I trade 2 positions at a disaster stop of 15pip ( 2X15 =30) @2.5 % of my account.Looking to one day trade it at 5% of the account but will have to get there slowly

Just my babels - Badly calculated risks spell disaster no matter what industry or environment

PS- Corrected all my grammar mistakes

--- 帖子 #2393 ---
Hi jtrade4u,

Bit late replying as busy weekend and only just saw your post.

You can put a 15 min cci on your 1 min screen very easily, its just a matter of a mathematical calculation. I use a 14 period CCI on my 1 min timeframe so thats my base CCI period, now if I want a 14 period 15min CCI on my 1 min chart as above then all I do is times 14 (cci period) by the timeframe I want, in this case 15 min so 14 x 15 = 210.

Then I just put a cci indy on 1 min timeframe set to 210. Its that simple and of course if I want to see the 1 hour CCI under that then its 14x60=840.Example of such a chart below the idea is very similar to the guys here where you trade in the same direction as the higher timeframes when the 1 min CCI pulls back against the 15 and 1 hour trends "hit it" so as chart below shows 1 hr and 15 min CCIs are trading down so sell any 1 min CCI signals.

Hope that helps?

By the way I am soon gonna start my own Trading Systems thread based around these ideas, hopefully monday time permitting, so if you're interested in this idea keep an eye out for it.

Heres my CCI indicator too just n case you haven't already got it.

--- 帖子 #2395 ---
Hi

Well to answer your first question I think its more about a straight through broker than a market maker but thats just my opinion.

As for your other question, well, I would say follow the 15 min CCI if trading the 1 min chart.

You also need to understand how the guy who designed the CCI indicator wanted it to work. Basically anything over 100 level is considered a strong trend and you should trade in that direction so if the 15 min CCI (210) is above the 100 level then look to take the 1 min cci (14) signals.

Let me give you some examples see chart below where the 15 min CCI is over -100 level then the 1 min CCI signals are pretty good, one proviso I tend to use is if selling 1 min CCIs then the signal you're taking should be level with or lower than the previous cci signal.

I also look to sell the 1 min signals once the the 15min CCI moves below the +100 level but moving downwards. Just make sure the 1 min CCI signals are level or lower than the previous one. EG only sell double tops or lower highs.As you can see out of the 8 signals 7 are winners and just 1 loser.

Good enough for an edge I'd say wouldn't you??

--- 帖子 #2411 ---
Hi maxs2002

If you like using the 14 period on your base chart then just times it by the timeframe you want above it. EG 14 x 5 = 70.

But to be honest I find it works best when you maintain an approx ratio of 15 to 1 between the time frames so I recommend as follows for each timeframe:

trading 1 min use 15 min as master (14 and 210)

trading 5 min use 1hr as master (14 and 168)

trading 15 min use 4hr as master (14 and 224)

trading 1hr use daily as master (14 and 336)

trading 4hr use weekly as master ( 14 and 504)

trading daily use monthly as master (14 and 350)

Its not an exact science but the logic behind it is that the momentum runs on say a daily chart are a down trend on the hrly chart so if daily pair falling off the page then sell the pullbacks(-100 CCI signals) on the hrly chart.

The single most important thing though is that you identify a strong trend before trading any pair as you will find momentum indicators are fairly accurate in a strong trending pair. eg top of the top 8 trenders indy.

Then look at hrly chart and sell the pullbacks against the trend.Of course all trends come to an end at sometime so you are almost guaranteed a loser at the end but stop taking the hrly cci's when daily CCI crosses down from the -100 level as trend is weakening.

Its all about momentum for me, look at attached chart shows EURAUD as top of the daily trenders so sell every 100cci signal thats over 100 and either a double top or Lower High. Use HA candle colour change as confirmation for entry.

Anyway will shortly start my own thread on this system as starting to hog Roois thread and thats simply bad etiquette so will be moving on soon. Apologies Rooi.

--- 帖子 #2560 ---
This is very off subject but this is for everyone's own knowledge.  My friend and I  hired a programmer on the Mq4 Mq5  website  where programmers will bid for various jobs once an MT4 user  posts his requests. When completed you will test the EA to your liking and specifications and only then will the payment process be completed.  Its like an escrow account where funds  will be held and released.  We never paid more then $50 dollars for a completed  EA however the more advanced it is, it could cost more.

Hi everybody.

Im new to this thread and would like to know what you guys think about my last trade.

I use Genesis system for entries and Babon system for exits.

Trading TF is M1 and M5 but mostly M1

So heres the trade...

1.

Price is near daily R1 and it seems to lose bullish momentum because it couldnt go much higher.

Stoch M5 just crossed and moving down. Stoch M15 didnt give any signals for going down.

Was to impatient and entered to early.

2.

Stop loss is above the yellow line (ADR)

Price is exhausted near ADR and is not able to move higher.

TMA H1 beyond TMA H4 which means we will have a pull back soon.

3.

A good short enter would be here in my opinion.

4.

PA movement wasnt that good so i exited when price almost touched the TMA M15 line (red dotted line)

Result: 13 Pips

Best regards.
